[2021/2/22-11:13-input]	 
[2021/2/22-11:13-clip]	 function wobblyFilter(magnitude: number) {
	const displacementSprite = PIXI.Sprite.from('displacement_map')
	const filter = new PIXI.filters.DisplacementFilter(displacementSprite, magnitude)
	// not a fan of this, as removal of filter.scale is done elsewhere (handleBuffChange in buff.client.ts)
	simpleAnimation_addPropertyAnimation(filter.scale, 'x', (t) => Math.sin(t) * magnitude)
	simpleAnimation_addPropertyAnimation(filter.scale, 'y', (t) => Math.sin(t * 1.1 + 0.2) * magnitude)
	return filter
}

			let movementSpeedBuff = 0
			let attackRateBuff = 0

			if (buff.appliedTo instanceof ServerPlayer) {
				movementSpeedBuff = -0.12
				attackRateBuff = -0.15
			} else if (buff.appliedTo.enemyType === EnemyType.BOSS) {
				movementSpeedBuff = -0.12
				attackRateBuff = -0.15
			} else {
				// normal enemies and champions
				movementSpeedBuff = -0.3
				attackRateBuff = -0.15
			}

			buff.state = {
				bonus1: buff.appliedTo.statList.addStatBonus('movementSpeed', StatOperatorType.MULTIPLY, movementSpeedBuff),
				bonus2: buff.appliedTo.statList.addStatBonus('attackRate', StatOperatorType.MULTIPLY, attackRateBuff),
			}
		},
		wearOffFn: (buff: Buff) => {
			buff.state.bonus1.remove()
			buff.state.bonus2.remove()

[2021/2/22-14:38-clip]	 			let targetHealthPercent: percentage = 0

			// do stack checks, possibly modify stats/apply stun and store changes in buff.state
			if (buff.appliedTo instanceof ServerPlayer) {
				targetHealthPercent = 0.3
			} else if (buff.appliedTo.enemyType === EnemyType.BOSS) {
				targetHealthPercent = 0.02
			} else if (buff.appliedTo.enemyType === EnemyType.CHAMPION) {
				targetHealthPercent = 0.1
			} else if (buff.appliedTo.enemyType === EnemyType.BASIC) {
				targetHealthPercent = 0.3
			} else {
				logger.error(`unknown enemy type: ${buff.appliedTo.enemyType}`)
				targetHealthPercent = 0.3
			}

			const resistStacks = Buff.getBuffStacks(buff.appliedTo, BuffIdentifier.StunResist)

			const lightningResist = Math.clamp(buff.appliedTo.statList.getStat('lightningResist'))
			const stunDuration = BuffData.map.get(BuffIdentifier.Stun).duration * (1 - lightningResist)
			const maxHealth = buff.appliedTo.maxHealth
			let threshold = (maxHealth * targetHealthPercent) + (maxHealth * 0.3 * resistStacks)

			addToElementDebugString(`   adding shock stasks:${buff.stacks.toFixed(1)} threshold:${threshold.toFixed(1)}\n`)
			while (buff.stacks >= threshold) {
				buff.stacks -= threshold

				Buff.apply(BuffIdentifier.StunResist, buff.owner, buff.appliedTo)

				threshold += (maxHealth * 0.3) // increase theshold on each stun

				const stun = Buff.apply(BuffIdentifier.Stun, buff.owner, buff.appliedTo, undefined, stunDuration)
				addToElementDebugString(`   ***STUN stunDuration:${stunDuration.toFixed(0)} actualDuration=${(stun.expiresAtTime - highResolutionTimestamp()).toFixed(0)}***   shock stacks after:${buff.stacks.toFixed(1)}\n`)
			}
